-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Important notes:

 Certain weapons can only be equipped by one or two characters.

 Range:   * Breaker weapons are ranged weapons and can hit any target within 
            the radius of their range.

        ** Shotgun and Quinqu Rain's attack range spreads out like a cone in
           front of them.

       *** Scythes hit the person in front of the target, 
           as well as the two enemies to the left and right of them.
